I have noticed that using it in circular movements as described in the booklet actually makes it more efficient - surprising since my other one has the same top/mechanism but didnt need all that.   122. Edit! 04/17/2017<br />I have owned this epilator for about 6 years now and it's still going strong. I no longer use it on my legs, though, so I wanted to address the reasons why in this review. This thing works really well on coarser hair (for me, that means under arms and bikini line). It does not do so well with fine hair. I was experiencing horrific and numerous ingrown hairs on my legs, which had never happened to me before - the finer hairs were apparently just breaking off under the skin rather than being removed at the root. I finally gave up and went back to shaving my legs but I'm still using the epilator for my underarms and bikini line. These areas have become almost completely desensitized to the initial pain I experienced when I first started using the epilator, and the hair growth itself is much sparser and seems to grow more slowly. Overall, I still rate it 4 stars but I wasn't able to chuck the razers completely. If you're tired of the expense of shaving, check out dollar shave club - because the blades are so affordable and they ship straight to my house, I don't feel like I have to use a blade until it's completely dull and rubbing my skin raw - in turn, I experience less razor burn and smoother skin.<br /><br />--------------------------------<br />I purchased this epilator from Target after reading some of the reviews about various brands and types of epilators here on Amazon.com (I didn't want to pay shipping, and this one wasn't available through Prime.)<br /><br />Although there weren't many reviews at the time I purchased the Remington EP6025, I was sold on the cordless function of this device.<br /><br />This is my FIRST epilator, so I am not able to provide any side-by-side comparisons. (I've used home-wax strips on a couple of occasions, but was relatively new to ripping hair out of my body.)<br /><br />All that being said, here are some observations after owning the device for a little over a month:<br /><br />1) This can be used with/without the cord, (which I didn't know when I bought it and turned out to be a plus.) When the battery starts to lose its charge, you can just find an outlet and keep on going. This differs from a number of trimmers/shavers I have owned in the past that can only function when the battery is charged (and must be placed in a &#34;charging station&#34; to recharge,) leaving you a partially hairy monster if you don't finish the job before the battery dies.<br /><br />2) It is comfortable to hold. Not too heavy, and not so light that it feels cheap and flimsy.<br /><br />3) There is NO way you can pinch your skin. When you press this epilator too firmly against your skin, the tweezers stop rotating. This is something I really appreciate because I'm prone to nicking myself with electric shavers and trimmers.<br /><br />4) There are two speeds. I began by using the lower speed on my legs, found that I was perfectly okay with the sensation of ripping the hair out by the roots (kind of a tingling, burning sensation at times, and almost feels like tiny shocks, especially behind the knees.) I was quickly able to speed it up, but noticed that if my hair was longer than a 1/4 inch, it either hurt a little more, or simply broke at the surface of the skin.) The breakage didn't seem to happen at the lower speed. The lower speed is also better for courser hair (under-arms, bikini area.)<br /><br />5) The battery didn't last long enough the first time I used it (TOO HAIRY!) but, as I mentioned above, I simply plugged it in and kept at it. Now that I'm in &#34;touch-up mode&#34; the battery life is fine for my needs.<br /><br />6) Exfoliation is KEY. I have noticed a couple ingrown hairs (just below the surface, and easily removed) but as long as I exfoliate daily, I haven't seen any nightmarish ingrown hairs as described by some people reviewing other epilators.<br /><br />7) My armpits have never looked better. YES, it HURTS! But it's a productive pain, and totally worth it. I was unable to have smooth armpits prior to buying this epilator because shaving led to horrible ingrown hairs, raw skin, and those dark roots right under the surface of my skin, even right after shaving. Now, my underarm skin is smooth, comfortable, and I have way more confidence wearing tank tops and sleeveless shirts.<br /><br />I'm very happy with this purchase, and I will provide updates if for some reason the thing just falls apart.<br /><br />**UPDATE 02/10/2012<br />This product has significanly slowed the hair growth on my legs and underarms- I have experienced more ingrown hairs on my legs, but always just under the surface, never the crazy, inflamed scary ones you hear about... I usually use this on my legs every couple of months, shaving in between if I must-- I have found that you get more bang for your buck if you wait through several hair growth cycles (these obnoxious little hairs grow at different rates...) then the re-growth is slowed to the 2 weeks the product description boasts... The battery is pretty much a non issue now and a useless feature, since I don't leave it plugged in to charge- I grab it out of the drawer without planning ahead, so I have to leave it plugged in while I use it.<br /><br />Hope this helps!hose dark roots right under the surface of my skin, even right after shaving. Now, my underarm skin is smooth, comfortable, and I have way more confidence wearing tank tops and sleeveless shirts. I'm very happy with this purchase, and I will provide updates if for some reason the thing just falls apart. **UPDATE 02/10/2012 This product has significanly slowed the hair growth on my legs and underarms- I have experienced more ingrown hairs on my legs, but always just under the surface, never the crazy, inflamed scary ones you hear about... I usually use this on my legs every couple of months, shaving in between if I must-- I have found that you get more bang for your buck if you wait through several hair growth cycles (these obnoxious little hairs grow at different rates...) then the re-growth is slowed to the 2 weeks the product description boasts... The battery is pretty much a non issue now and a useless feature, since I don't leave it plugged in to charge- I grab it out of the drawer without planning ahead, so I have to leave it plugged in while I use it.   238. I was so afraid of this thing it took me months to actually use it. Now it's old news and I celebrate mustache Monday. As a woman in menopause I don't relish the idea of having a mustache as noticeable as my husband's. That said there is a bit of an art to using this scary thing. First and foremost this machine is actually multiple TWEEZERS! Don't smash it against your skin. When you press it against your skin it flattens the hair and it can't grab it. Make sure that it is fully charged. Start with the lower speed until you get the hang of it. Yeah yeah it hurts, it makes your eyes water but the more you do it the easier it gets. I can now go high speed and have mustache and those lovely chin hairs done in less than 2 minutes. Make sure that you keep the tweezers clean. When you pull hair out by the root you get skin with it, whether it's microscopic dry skin or the root itself, it sticks to the tweezers which keeps them from closing properly and pulling the hairs out efficiently. My fabulous husband bought me this wonderful magnifying glass with a light in it from Ultra Optix, it shows up a lot of ugly including fabric fibers, skin, hair. It shows up what you don't want to know but really need to know. So clean it. Make sure that the epilator is NOT on the charger. Remove the tweezer head from the body of the epilator. I use an old soft toothbrush and warm water to scrub mine then inspect it with the magnifier until it's clean. Pat it dry with a clean towel, don't rub it, you just got the fibers out. Let it dry for a couple of minutes, put it back together and turn it on high to get it a bit dryer then leave it for about 30 minutes before you plug it back in.

  274. This was my first experience with epilating so i was very skeptical about spending too much in case i hated it. Remington has always been a trusted brand for me and this one was mid price range so i went for it. I normally shave my legs every single day and have stubble within 8 hours. Waxing was okay except i had to wait for the hair to be fully grown out! that doesnt work during summer months! So epilating seemed to be a medium-ground solution. Very disapointed at first. The pain was ridiculous! And the results, not what i was thinking! Not at all like a nice smooth shave! And the time? oh geez.. at LEAST an hour! I tried epilating every day with zero improvment. It was almost like the hair was just breaking off just above the skin and then too short for the machine to grab ahold again. After several hours of reading reviews, changing my technique, and downing many glasses of wine to endure the pain, here is the routine i follow now: Exfoliate with shower mittens (and i mean a good good scrubbing), well dried off and NO lotion (not even numbing cream, tried it, no bueno), starting at my ankles i work my way up in the opposite direction the hair grows, in areas where the hair seems to grow in ALL directions i use small circular motions. I do not move on from one particular area until i can no longer feel any pulling. Full legs took me about 45 mins and sometimes would shave in the morning to get those tiny ones i missed. Fast forward 3 months... there is hardly any pain anymore! yay! Except the back of my knees is a teeny bit sensitve, but NOTHING like at first! I now only do this once a week, takes about 20-30 mins. I no longer shave in between sessions now that ive caught the hair cycle just right and the hair grows back soft instead of prickly. I have course hair on my lower legs and fine blonde hair on my thighs and this works great for both areas. The blonde hair is just hard to see but of course is still felt! I give this product 4 out of 5 stars only because the battery life is kinda weak. If i charge it all night, I get one leg done and it starts to get weak. I no longer charge it. I just plug it in and never use it as \\"cordless\\". Legs are the only area i have used the Remington, but with the variety of hair its proven to master, i am confident it would work great anywhere else. Patience is key!
